		icon = gold_standard

		x = -19
		y = 2
		relative_position_id = MOR_the_moroccan_economy

		cost = 6.8

		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL FOCUS_FILTER_STABILITY }
		prerequisite = { focus = MOR_the_bounty_of_the_mountains }

		available = { }
		# bypass = { }
		# cancel = { }

		# select_effect = { }
		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus MOR_exploit_gold_reserves"
			# TODO: Add a check here that if you are a more authoritarian Monarch you gain some for your personal use
			# TODO: Change this to the most appropriate state
			set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -7.5 }
			modify_treasury_effect = yes
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = MOR_aggressive_resource_exploitation }
				add_resource = {
					type = chromium
					amount = 14
					state = 1176
				}
				add_stability = -0.02
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = MOR_corrupted_aggressive_resource_exploitation }
				add_resource = {
					type = chromium
					amount = 14
					state = 1176
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_resource = {
					type = chromium
					amount = 8
					state = 1176
				}
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				check_variable = { resource_consumed@chromium > resource_produced@chromium }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				check_variable = { interest_rate > 10.99 }
			}
		}
	}
